1257 <i>

1258

1259 Updated on May 6, 2020.&nbsp;

1267 <p>

1268<img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-16951 lazyload" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAA14AAAExAQAAAABEnk75AAAAAnRSTlMAAHaTzTgAAAA3SURBVHja7cEBDQAAAMKg909tDwcUAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAMCxAYHdAAFAJYhiAAAAAElFTkSuQmCC" alt="marijuana for tendinitis" width="862" height="305" data-src="https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-for-tendinitis.jpg?strip=all&lossy=1&resize=862%2C305&ssl=1" loading="lazy" data-srcset="https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-for-tendinitis.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 862w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-for-tendinitis-200x71.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 200w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-for-tendinitis-300x106.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-for-tendinitis-768x272.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-for-tendinitis-49x17.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 49w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-for-tendinitis.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;w=384 384w" data-sizes="auto" />

1269<noscript>

1270<img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-16951 lazy" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20862%20305'%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-for-tendinitis.jpg?strip=all&lossy=1&resize=862%2C305&ssl=1" alt="marijuana for tendinitis" width="862" height="305" data-srcset="https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-for-tendinitis.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 862w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-for-tendinitis-200x71.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 200w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-for-tendinitis-300x106.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-for-tendinitis-768x272.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-for-tendinitis-49x17.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 49w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-for-tendinitis.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;w=384 384w" data-sizes="(max-width: 862px) 100vw, 862px" data-eio="l" />

1271</noscript>

1272<br />

1273

1274Tendinitis is a common, yet painful, tendon condition that can be acute or chronic. Almost anyone can develop this condition, although it&#8217;s most common among &#8220;weekend warriors&#8221; who exercise or play hard on Saturdays and Sundays. It’s also prevalent in athletes and people with jobs involving repetitive motions.</p>

1275

1276<p>

1277If you have tenderness and pain in your joints when you move, lift or walk, you may be suffering from tendinitis. Here&#8217;s what you should know about what causes it and how it&#8217;s treated, including using marijuana for tendinitis.</p>

1278

1562

1563<h2>

1564What Is Tendinitis?</h2>

1565

1566<p>

1567Tendons are thick cords of connective tissue attaching muscle to bone. They work as a pulley to help muscles move joints, but sometimes the tendons become inflamed and tender, developing into a condition called tendinitis. This ailment can happen anywhere on the body with a tendon.</p>

1568

1569<h2>

1570Causes of Tendinitis</h2>

1571

1572<p>

1573Sometimes tendinitis is the result of a sudden injury, but it&#8217;s far more likely to result from repetitive motions due to a hobby or job. Someone who spends too much time typing, for example, can develop tendinitis of the elbow or wrist. Runners may get tendinitis of the Achilles tendon.</p>

1574

1575<p>

1576People who have poor posture, osteoarthritis or diabetes are prone to tendinitis. Sometimes, certain medication can trigger a tendinitis injury.</p>

1577

1578<p>

1579You may be at a higher risk of developing tendinitis if you:</p>

1580

1581<ul>

1582

1583<li>

1584Are more than 40 years old. As your tendons age, they become less elastic and more likely to tear under stress.</li>

1585

1586<li>

1587Participate in specific sports like baseball, tennis, golf, running, swimming or bowling</li>

1588

1589<li>

1590Have a job that involves reaching overhead frequently, repetitive movements or awkward positions</li>

1591

1592</ul>

1593

1594<p>

1595You can prevent tendinitis by using the proper technique when performing job activities and repetitive movements, especially during sports.</p>

1596

1597<h2>

1598Types of Tendinitis</h2>

1599

1600<p>

1601Because tendinitis refers to inflammation of connective tissue, health care experts divided it into many subtypes based on the affected tendon. Specific types of the condition are classified by the activity causing the strain or the part of the body affected. The following are the five most common forms of tendinitis.</p>

1602

1603<ol>

1604

1605<li>

1606<strong>

1607Tennis elbow: </strong>

1608Also known as elbow tendinitis, this form of tendinitis gets its name because it affects the tendon used repetitively in tennis. Tennis elbow results in inflammation of the tendon in the outside of the elbow that allows the wrist and fingers to extend.</li>

1609

1610<li>

1611<strong>

1612Golfer&#8217;s elbow: </strong>

1613This is another type of tendinitis affecting the elbow, although golfer&#8217;s elbow impacts the tendon of the inner side of the elbow. This type of tendinitis can cause pain in the wrist and forearm. Golfer’s elbow isn’t limited to people who golf. Anyone can develop it, even people who never play golf. And, even though it’s called “golfer’s elbow,” tennis players can experience it too.</li>

1614

1615<li>

1616<strong>

1617Rotator cuff tendinitis: </strong>

1618The rotator cuff of the shoulder has four tendons assisting with shoulder movement. Tendinitis can affect any of these tendons. Sometimes tendinitis of the shoulder is the result of repetitive movements, but it can also be the result of a traumatic injury.</li>

1619

1620<li>

1621<strong>

1622Achilles tendinitis: </strong>

1623This type of tendinitis affects the Achilles tendon connecting the heel bone to the calf muscles. This overuse injury becomes more common with age, but jumpers, runners and many other athletes are at a higher risk. The Achilles is a large tendon, and when injured, can take months to heal. If you completely tear the Achilles, <a href="https://www.sportsmd.com/sports-injuries/hip-thigh-injuries/achilles-tendon-injury/">

1624you may need surgery, and rehabilitation</a>

1625 can take up to nine months.</li>

1626

1627<li>

1628<strong>

1629Biceps tendinitis: </strong>

1630This form of tendinitis affects the biceps tendon connecting the shoulder bone to the biceps muscle. Biceps tendinitis is often the result of overuse or repetitive movements of the shoulder. It can occur alongside rotator cuff tendinitis.</li>

1631

1632<li>

1633<strong>

1634Jumper&#8217;s knee:  </strong>

1635More common in people who regularly play sports involving jumping, such as basketball players, this condition causes inflamed or torn tendons in the knee.</li>

1636

1637</ol>

1638

1639<p>

1640<img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-16952 lazyload" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAA14AAAExAQAAAABEnk75AAAAAnRSTlMAAHaTzTgAAAA3SURBVHja7cEBDQAAAMKg909tDwcUAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAMCxAYHdAAFAJYhiAAAAAElFTkSuQmCC" alt="66" width="862" height="305" data-src="https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-tennis-elbow.jpg?strip=all&lossy=1&resize=862%2C305&ssl=1" loading="lazy" data-srcset="https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-tennis-elbow.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 862w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-tennis-elbow-200x71.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 200w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-tennis-elbow-300x106.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-tennis-elbow-768x272.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-tennis-elbow-49x17.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 49w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-tennis-elbow.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;w=384 384w" data-sizes="auto" />

1641<noscript>

1642<img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-16952 lazy" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20862%20305'%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-tennis-elbow.jpg?strip=all&lossy=1&resize=862%2C305&ssl=1" alt="66" width="862" height="305" data-srcset="https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-tennis-elbow.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 862w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-tennis-elbow-200x71.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 200w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-tennis-elbow-300x106.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-tennis-elbow-768x272.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-tennis-elbow-49x17.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 49w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-tennis-elbow.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;w=384 384w" data-sizes="(max-width: 862px) 100vw, 862px" data-eio="l" />

1643</noscript>

1644</p>

1645

1646<h2>

1647Symptoms of Tendinitis</h2>

1648

1649<p>

1650Tendinitis usually causes pain just outside the joint or where the tendon attaches to the bone. Some swelling may be apparent, but you’ll likely have tenderness and pain feeling like a dull ache when you move the joint or body part. You may also experience a loss of motion in the affected joint, especially the shoulder. This condition is called frozen shoulder or adhesive capsulitis.</p>

1651

1652<p>

1653The difficulties you encounter with the symptoms of tendinitis depend on the type. For instance, someone with golfer’s elbow may have trouble shaking hands or gripping a doorknob, whereas a person with Achilles tendinitis may find it painful to walk up and down stairs.</p>

1654

1655<h2>

1656History of Tendinitis</h2>

1657

1658<p>

1659Surprisingly, tendinitis went undocumented until the 1940s, when <a href="http://marcellobaldacchini.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/07/histopathology-of-common-tendinopathies.pdf">

1660German workers first used the term</a>

1661 to describe injuries. The condition didn&#8217;t receive much attention until the 1980s, when it was used to describe a <a href="https://academic.oup.com/rheumatology/article/47/10/1444/1787695">

1662non-inflammatory condition</a>

1663 of the tendons. At this point, Scandinavian authors first used physical therapy to treat the condition, with good results.</p>

1664

1665<p>

1666Dr. Janet Travell pioneered and popularized the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Janet_G._Travell">

1667use of corticosteroid injections</a>

1668, now a common therapy for tendon pain.</p>

1669

1670<h2>

1671Effects of Tendinitis</h2>

1672

1673<p>

1674Tendinitis can be an excruciating condition, making it difficult to perform basic tasks, work and enjoy a full range of motion. If tendinitis continues without proper treatment, you may struggle to perform your favorite hobbies, enjoy sports or even do something as simple as opening a door. These limitations may also lead to depression and difficulty sleeping, especially if the pain keeps you up at night.</p>

1675

1676<p>

1677If you don&#8217;t seek treatment, tendinitis can become chronic. Long-term tendinitis increases the risk of a tendon rupture, which may require surgery. Irritation and <a href="https://www.marijuanadoctors.com/conditions/inflammation/">

1678inflammation</a>

1679 continuing for weeks or months can also lead to tendinosis, a degenerative condition damaging the tendon and causing abnormal blood vessel growth. The <a href="https://www.marijuanadoctors.com/conditions/chronic-pain/">

1680chronic pain</a>

1681 involved in long-term tendinitis may interfere with sleeping, daily life activities, depression and reduced quality of life.</p>

1682

1683<h2>

1684Statistics of Tendinitis</h2>

1685

1686<ul>

1687

1688<li>

1689Every year, more than <a href="https://www.piedmont.org/living-better/are-you-texting-your-way-to-tendonitis">

169070,000 people miss work</a>

1691 due to tendinitis, according to the U.S. Bureau of Labor Statistics.</li>

1692

1693<li>

1694About <a href="http://onlinelibrary.wiley.com/doi/10.1002/1097-0274(200103)39:3%3C328::AID-AJIM1021%3E3.0.CO;2-I/abstract">

169528 percent of cases of</a>

1696tendinitis are work-related, according to a study published in 2001.</li>

1697

1698<li>

1699Runners are at high risk for tendinitis of the Achilles tendon. While <a href="https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/7809555">

170070 to 90 percent have a complete comeback</a>

1701 after surgery, 3 to 5 percent must abandon their running career after an Achilles tendon injury.</li>

1702

1703<li>

1704About <a href="https://www.painfreelivinglife.com/pain-conditions/tendonitis/tendonitis-symptoms-types/">

170515 percent of all running injuries</a>

1706 involve Achilles tendinitis.</li>

1707

1708<li>

1709Rotator cuff tendinitis is the most common form of the condition, affecting about <a href="https://www.painfreelivinglife.com/pain-conditions/tendonitis/tendonitis-symptoms-types/">

1710one in 50 adults</a>

1711.</li>

1712

1713</ul>

1714

1715<p>

1716<img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-16954 lazyload" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAA14AAAExAQAAAABEnk75AAAAAnRSTlMAAHaTzTgAAAA3SURBVHja7cEBDQAAAMKg909tDwcUAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAMCxAYHdAAFAJYhiAAAAAElFTkSuQmCC" alt="marijuana achilles injury" width="862" height="305" data-src="https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-achilles-injry.jpg?strip=all&lossy=1&resize=862%2C305&ssl=1" loading="lazy" data-srcset="https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-achilles-injry.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 862w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-achilles-injry-200x71.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 200w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-achilles-injry-300x106.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-achilles-injry-768x272.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-achilles-injry-49x17.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 49w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-achilles-injry.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;w=384 384w" data-sizes="auto" />

1717<noscript>

1718<img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-16954 lazy" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20862%20305'%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-achilles-injry.jpg?strip=all&lossy=1&resize=862%2C305&ssl=1" alt="marijuana achilles injury" width="862" height="305" data-srcset="https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-achilles-injry.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 862w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-achilles-injry-200x71.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 200w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-achilles-injry-300x106.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-achilles-injry-768x272.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-achilles-injry-49x17.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 49w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-achilles-injry.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;w=384 384w" data-sizes="(max-width: 862px) 100vw, 862px" data-eio="l" />

1719</noscript>

1720</p>

1721

1722<h2>

1723Current Treatments Available for Tendinitis and Their Side Effects</h2>

1724

1725<p>

1726The good news is, tendinitis can usually be treated effectively with few side effects. Typically, your primary care physician can treat a mild case of tendinitis. In more moderate to severe cases, you may need to see a physical therapist, orthopedist or rheumatologist for a definitive diagnosis and treatment plan.</p>

1727

1728<p>

1729To diagnose tendinitis, your doctor will perform one or more of the following:</p>

1730

1731<ul>

1732

1733<li>

1734Visually inspect the area for swelling</li>

1735

1736<li>

1737Touch the area to see if it has swollen</li>

1738

1739<li>

1740Order X-rays to rule out other issues besides tendinitis</li>

1741

1742<li>

1743Order an MRI to show where the location of the swollen tendon</li>

1744

1745<li>

1746Retrieve fluid from the swollen area to check for infection</li>

1747

1748<li>

1749Inject an anesthetic to determine if it eliminates the pain</li>

1750

1751</ul>

1752

1753<h3>

1754Acute Tendinitis Treatment</h3>

1755

1756<p>

1757After symptoms begin, you should avoid any activities worsening the problem and allow the tendon to rest. You may apply ice for acute tendon injuries, but you don&#8217;t typically use it for long-term tendinitis recovery. If you suffered an injury, doctors advice you to ice the area for a day or two. OTC anti-inflammatory drugs can also help.</p>

1758

1759<h3>

1760Beyond Acute Tendinitis Treatment</h3>

1761

1762<p>

1763If tendinitis does not improve within a week, your physician may recommend physical therapy or corticosteroid injections. Physical therapy, which includes gentle strengthening and stretching exercises, can improve your range of motion. Physical therapy may also include splinting the affected area and soft-tissue massage. Your doctor or physical therapist may also recommend banding, compressing, splinting or bracing your injured area.</p>

1764

1765<p>

1766<img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-16955 lazyload" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAA14AAAExAQAAAABEnk75AAAAAnRSTlMAAHaTzTgAAAA3SURBVHja7cEBDQAAAMKg909tDwcUAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAMCxAYHdAAFAJYhiAAAAAElFTkSuQmCC" alt="marijuana and steroids" width="862" height="305" data-src="https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-and-steroids.jpg?strip=all&lossy=1&resize=862%2C305&ssl=1" loading="lazy" data-srcset="https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-and-steroids.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 862w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-and-steroids-200x71.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 200w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-and-steroids-300x106.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-and-steroids-768x272.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-and-steroids-49x17.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 49w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-and-steroids.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;w=384 384w" data-sizes="auto" />

1767<noscript>

1768<img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-16955 lazy" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20862%20305'%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-and-steroids.jpg?strip=all&lossy=1&resize=862%2C305&ssl=1" alt="marijuana and steroids" width="862" height="305" data-srcset="https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-and-steroids.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 862w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-and-steroids-200x71.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 200w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-and-steroids-300x106.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-and-steroids-768x272.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-and-steroids-49x17.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;ssl=1 49w, https://cdnx.marijuanadoctors.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/marijuana-and-steroids.jpg?strip=all&amp;lossy=1&amp;w=384 384w" data-sizes="(max-width: 862px) 100vw, 862px" data-eio="l" />

1769</noscript>

1770</p>

1771

1772<p>

1773Corticosteroids can quickly reduce inflammation and pain in the area to speed healing. In rare cases of severe tendinitis, you may need surgery. If your physician recommends corticosteroids, you will use them on a very short-term basis, because they can come with many side effects. Long-term corticosteroid use can increase the risk of osteoporosis, high blood pressure, diabetes, infection and eye disorders.</p>

1774

1775<p>

1776With proper exercise and physical therapy, partially torn tendons may take several months to heal and restore their strength. You may need surgery for completely torn tendons.</p>
